## 1: Prompt 1

Optimize the substrate kernel in /workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p56/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round2/output_model_new.py

Use MFMA instructions `S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32` to do matrix multiplications and loads the data from global memory using vectorized loads S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4. The MFMA instruction computes 32x32x8 matmul cooperatively in a wave. Build larger tiles by issuing multiple MFMA instructions across K and output subtiles.

Stage A and B through LDS. Each thread loads operand fragments in 16-byte chunks. Treat each 16-byte fragment as `(4, S.u32)` and reinterpret it as `2 x (4, S.bf16)`. Feed both `(4, S.bf16)` halves into MFMA in natural order. The intended effect is a cooperative `32x32x16` accumulation from two natural MFMA steps. Do not add lane-dependent or K-dependent control flow to select halves.
  - The two `(4, S.bf16)` halves from one 16-byte LDS load collectively represent a swizzled `32x16` operand contribution with 4-column interleaving.
  - Consuming them in natural order must produce the same final C as a naive conceptual layout because operand pairings remain consistent under MFMA swizzle.

Scale the kernel from one wave to four waves without changing the MFMA per-wave invariant. Interpret the 4 warps as a 2 x 2 warp grid. Keep MFMA math identical per warp. Only add warp ownership offsets at operand fetch and output writeback.

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S


BATCH_SIZE = 128
INPUT_SIZE = 32768
HIDDEN_SIZE = 32768
TILE_M = 64
TILE_N = 64
TILE_K = 16
BLOCK_THREADS = 256


def _launch():
    return ((BATCH_SIZE // TILE_M, 1, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))


@substrate.jit
def fused_kernel(
    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    W: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, 1), S.bf16),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid & 63
    wave = tid >> 6
    warp_row = wave >> 1
    warp_col = wave & 1
    block_row = S.block_id(0) * TILE_M

    zero_i32 = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    zero_u32 = S.convert(0, S.u32)
    zero_f32 = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
    one_f32 = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)

    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2, S.i32))
    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2, S.i32))

    a_shared = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
    b_shared = S.make_shared((2, 64, 4), S.u32)
    c_shared = S.make_shared((TILE_M, TILE_N), S.f32)
    row_sums = S.make_shared((TILE_M,), S.f32)

    if tid < TILE_M:
        row_sums[tid] = zero_f32
    S.syncthreads()

    for n_tile in S.range(HIDDEN_SIZE // TILE_N):
        n0 = n_tile * TILE_N
        c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

        for k_tile in S.range(INPUT_SIZE // TILE_K):
            k0 = k_tile * TILE_K

            if tid < 128:
                a_row = tid >> 1
                a_half = tid & 1
                a_tile = a_row >> 5
                a_local = a_row & 31
                a_offset = S.convert(((block_row + a_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k0 + a_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
                a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero_i32, a_offset, 0)
                if a_half == 0:
                    a_shared[a_tile, a_local, 0] = a_pack[0]
                    a_shared[a_tile, a_local, 1] = a_pack[1]
                    a_shared[a_tile, a_local + 32, 0] = a_pack[2]
                    a_shared[a_tile, a_local + 32, 1] = a_pack[3]
                else:
                    a_shared[a_tile, a_local, 2] = a_pack[0]
                    a_shared[a_tile, a_local, 3] = a_pack[1]
                    a_shared[a_tile, a_local + 32, 2] = a_pack[2]
                    a_shared[a_tile, a_local + 32, 3] = a_pack[3]

            if tid >= 128:
                b_tid = tid - 128
                b_col = b_tid >> 1
                b_half = b_tid & 1
                b_tile = b_col >> 5
                b_local = b_col & 31
                b_offset = S.convert(((n0 + b_col) * INPUT_SIZE + k0 + b_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
                b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero_i32, b_offset, 0)
                if b_half == 0:
                    b_shared[b_tile, b_local, 0] = b_pack[0]
                    b_shared[b_tile, b_local, 1] = b_pack[1]
                    b_shared[b_tile, b_local + 32, 0] = b_pack[2]
                    b_shared[b_tile, b_local + 32, 1] = b_pack[3]
                else:
                    b_shared[b_tile, b_local, 2] = b_pack[0]
                    b_shared[b_tile, b_local, 3] = b_pack[1]
                    b_shared[b_tile, b_local + 32, 2] = b_pack[2]
                    b_shared[b_tile, b_local + 32, 3] = b_pack[3]

            S.syncthreads()

            a_frag = S.view(a_shared[warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
            b_frag = S.view(b_shared[warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

            c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[0], b_frag[0], c_lane)
            c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag[1], b_frag[1], c_lane)

            S.syncthreads()

        local_col = warp_col * 32 + (lane & 31)
        global_col = n0 + local_col
        bias = S.convert(BIAS0[global_col], S.f32)
        row_lane_bit = lane >> 5

        for slot in S.range(16):
            local_row = warp_row * 32 + (slot & 3) + 4 * row_lane_bit + 8 * (slot >> 2)
            value = c_lane[slot] + bias
            sigmoid = one_f32 / (one_f32 + S.exp(-value))
            c_shared[local_row, local_col] = sigmoid

        S.syncthreads()

        if tid < TILE_M:
            partial = row_sums[tid]
            for col in S.range(TILE_N):
                partial += c_shared[tid, col]
            row_sums[tid] = partial

        S.syncthreads()

    if tid < TILE_M:
        Y[block_row + tid, 0] = S.convert(row_sums[tid], S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, input_size, hidden_size):
        super().__init__()
        self.linear = nn.Linear(input_size, hidden_size)
        self._weight_cache = None
        self._weight_key = None
        self._bias_cache = None
        self._bias_key = None

    def _maybe_refresh_cache(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
        weight = self.linear.weight
        bias = self.linear.bias
        weight_key = (weight.data_ptr(), weight._version, x.device, torch.bfloat16)
        bias_key = (bias.data_ptr(), bias._version, x.device, torch.bfloat16)

        if self._weight_key != weight_key:
            self._weight_cache = weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16).contiguous()
            self._weight_key = weight_key
        if self._bias_key != bias_key:
            self._bias_cache = bias.to(device=x.device, dtype=torch.bfloat16).contiguous()
            self._bias_key = bias_key
        return self._weight_cache, self._bias_cache

    def forward(self, x):
        if tuple(x.shape) != (BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE) or x.dtype != torch.bfloat16:
            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")
        w, bias = self._maybe_refresh_cache(x)
        y = torch.empty((BATCH_SIZE, 1), device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
        fused_kernel[_launch](x.contiguous(), w, bias, y)
        return y

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_16x16x16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((4,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.f16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)
    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_16x16x16_f16_f32(m_a[1], m_b[1], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane


@substrate.jit
def gemm_mfma_32x32x8_bf16(
    A: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    B: S.Tensor((64, 2), S.u32),
    C: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
):
    lane = S.thread_id(0)

    c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

    m_a = S.view(A[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))
    m_b = S.view(B[lane], S.Tensor((1, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(m_a[0], m_b[0], c_lane)

    C[lane] = c_lane

 def _launch():

+def _load_stage(x_rsrc, w_rsrc, a_shared, b_shared, stage, k0, n0, block_row, tid, zero_i32):
+    if tid < 128:
+        a_row = tid >> 1
+        a_half = tid & 1
+        a_tile = a_row >> 5
+        a_local = a_row & 31
+        a_offset = S.convert(((block_row + a_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k0 + a_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero_i32, a_offset, 0)
+        if a_half == 0:
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local, 0] = a_pack[0]
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local, 1] = a_pack[1]
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local + 32, 0] = a_pack[2]
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local + 32, 1] = a_pack[3]
+        else:
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local, 2] = a_pack[0]
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local, 3] = a_pack[1]
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local + 32, 2] = a_pack[2]
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local + 32, 3] = a_pack[3]
+
+    if tid >= 128:
+        b_tid = tid - 128
+        b_col = b_tid >> 1
+        b_half = b_tid & 1
+        b_tile = b_col >> 5
+        b_local = b_col & 31
+        b_offset = S.convert(((n0 + b_col) * INPUT_SIZE + k0 + b_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero_i32, b_offset, 0)
+        if b_half == 0:
+            b_shared[stage, b_tile, b_local, 0] = b_pack[0]
+            b_shared[stage, b_tile, b_local, 1] = b_pack[1]
+            b_shared[stage, b_tile, b_local + 32, 0] = b_pack[2]
+            b_shared[stage, b_tile, b_local + 32, 1] = b_pack[3]
+        else:
+            b_shared[stage, b_tile, b_local, 2] = b_pack[0]
+            b_shared[stage, b_tile, b_local, 3] = b_pack[1]
+            b_shared[stage, b_tile, b_local + 32, 2] = b_pack[2]
+            b_shared[stage, b_tile, b_local + 32, 3] = b_pack[3]

+def _load_stage(x_rsrc, w_rsrc, a_shared, b_shared, stage, k0, n0, block_row, tid, zero_i32):
+    if tid < 128:
+        a_row = tid >> 1
+        a_half = tid & 1
+        a_tile = a_row >> 5
+        a_local = a_row & 31
+        a_offset = S.convert(((block_row + a_row) * INPUT_SIZE + k0 + a_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
+        a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero_i32, a_offset, 0)
+        if a_half == 0:
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local, 0] = a_pack[0]
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local, 1] = a_pack[1]
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local + 32, 0] = a_pack[2]
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local + 32, 1] = a_pack[3]
+        else:
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local, 2] = a_pack[0]
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local, 3] = a_pack[1]
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local + 32, 2] = a_pack[2]
+            a_shared[stage, a_tile, a_local + 32, 3] = a_pack[3]
+

+        b_col = b_tid >> 1
+        b_half = b_tid & 1
+        b_tile = b_col >> 5

                a_local = a_row & 31
                a_offset = S.convert(((block_row + a_row) * INPUT_SIZE + next_k0 + a_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
                a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero_i32, a_offset, 0)
                if a_half == 0:
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local, 0] = a_pack[0]
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local, 1] = a_pack[1]
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local + 32, 0] = a_pack[2]
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local + 32, 1] = a_pack[3]
                else:
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local, 2] = a_pack[0]
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local, 3] = a_pack[1]
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local + 32, 2] = a_pack[2]
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local + 32, 3] = a_pack[3]

            if tid >= 128:
                b_tid = tid - 128
                b_col = b_tid >> 1
                b_half = b_tid & 1
                b_tile = b_col >> 5
                b_local = b_col & 31
                b_offset = S.convert(((n0 + b_col) * INPUT_SIZE + next_k0 + b_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
                b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero_i32, b_offset, 0)
                if b_half == 0:
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local, 0] = b_pack[0]
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local, 1] = b_pack[1]
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local + 32, 0] = b_pack[2]
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local + 32, 1] = b_pack[3]
                else:

                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local, 3] = b_pack[1]
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local + 32, 2] = b_pack[2]
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local + 32, 3] = b_pack[3]

            a_frag1 = S.view(a_shared[1, warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
            b_frag1 = S.view(b_shared[1, warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
            c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], c_lane)

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S


BATCH_SIZE = 128
INPUT_SIZE = 32768
HIDDEN_SIZE = 32768
TILE_M = 64
TILE_N = 64
TILE_K = 16
BLOCK_THREADS = 256
K_PAIR_TILES = TILE_K * 2
NUM_K_PAIRS = INPUT_SIZE // K_PAIR_TILES


def _launch():
    return ((BATCH_SIZE // TILE_M, 1, 1), (BLOCK_THREADS, 1, 1))


@substrate.jit
def fused_kernel(
    X: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    W: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE, INPUT_SIZE), S.bf16),
    BIAS0: S.Tensor((HIDDEN_SIZE,), S.bf16),
    Y: S.Tensor((BATCH_SIZE, 1), S.bf16),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    lane = tid & 63
    wave = tid >> 6
    warp_row = wave >> 1
    warp_col = wave & 1
    block_row = S.block_id(0) * TILE_M

    zero_i32 = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    zero_f32 = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
    one_f32 = S.convert(1.0, S.f32)

    x_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(X, S.convert(BATCH_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2, S.i32))
    w_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(W, S.convert(HIDDEN_SIZE * INPUT_SIZE * 2, S.i32))

    a_shared = S.make_shared((2, 2, 64, 4), S.u32)
    b_shared = S.make_shared((2, 2, 64, 4), S.u32)
    c_shared = S.make_shared((TILE_M, TILE_N), S.f32)
    row_sums = S.make_shared((TILE_M,), S.f32)

    if tid < TILE_M:
        row_sums[tid] = zero_f32
    S.syncthreads()

    for n_tile in S.range(HIDDEN_SIZE // TILE_N):
        n0 = n_tile * TILE_N
        c_lane = S.full((16,), 0.0, S.f32)

        if tid < 128:
            a_row = tid >> 1
            a_half = tid & 1
            a_tile = a_row >> 5
            a_local = a_row & 31

            a_offset0 = S.convert(((block_row + a_row) * INPUT_SIZE + a_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
            a_pack0 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero_i32, a_offset0, 0)
            if a_half == 0:
                a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local, 0] = a_pack0[0]
                a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local, 1] = a_pack0[1]
                a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local + 32, 0] = a_pack0[2]
                a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local + 32, 1] = a_pack0[3]
            else:
                a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local, 2] = a_pack0[0]
                a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local, 3] = a_pack0[1]
                a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local + 32, 2] = a_pack0[2]
                a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local + 32, 3] = a_pack0[3]

            a_offset1 = S.convert(((block_row + a_row) * INPUT_SIZE + TILE_K + a_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
            a_pack1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero_i32, a_offset1, 0)
            if a_half == 0:
                a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local, 0] = a_pack1[0]
                a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local, 1] = a_pack1[1]
                a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local + 32, 0] = a_pack1[2]
                a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local + 32, 1] = a_pack1[3]
            else:
                a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local, 2] = a_pack1[0]
                a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local, 3] = a_pack1[1]
                a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local + 32, 2] = a_pack1[2]
                a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local + 32, 3] = a_pack1[3]

        if tid >= 128:
            b_tid = tid - 128
            b_col = b_tid >> 1
            b_half = b_tid & 1
            b_tile = b_col >> 5
            b_local = b_col & 31

            b_offset0 = S.convert(((n0 + b_col) * INPUT_SIZE + b_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
            b_pack0 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero_i32, b_offset0, 0)
            if b_half == 0:
                b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local, 0] = b_pack0[0]
                b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local, 1] = b_pack0[1]
                b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local + 32, 0] = b_pack0[2]
                b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local + 32, 1] = b_pack0[3]
            else:
                b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local, 2] = b_pack0[0]
                b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local, 3] = b_pack0[1]
                b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local + 32, 2] = b_pack0[2]
                b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local + 32, 3] = b_pack0[3]

            b_offset1 = S.convert(((n0 + b_col) * INPUT_SIZE + TILE_K + b_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
            b_pack1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero_i32, b_offset1, 0)
            if b_half == 0:
                b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local, 0] = b_pack1[0]
                b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local, 1] = b_pack1[1]
                b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local + 32, 0] = b_pack1[2]
                b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local + 32, 1] = b_pack1[3]
            else:
                b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local, 2] = b_pack1[0]
                b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local, 3] = b_pack1[1]
                b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local + 32, 2] = b_pack1[2]
                b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local + 32, 3] = b_pack1[3]
        S.syncthreads()

        for k_pair in S.range(NUM_K_PAIRS - 1):
            a_frag0 = S.view(a_shared[0, warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
            b_frag0 = S.view(b_shared[0, warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
            c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], c_lane)
            c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[1], b_frag0[1], c_lane)

            next_k0 = (k_pair + 1) * K_PAIR_TILES
            if tid < 128:
                a_row = tid >> 1
                a_half = tid & 1
                a_tile = a_row >> 5
                a_local = a_row & 31
                a_offset = S.convert(((block_row + a_row) * INPUT_SIZE + next_k0 + a_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
                a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero_i32, a_offset, 0)
                if a_half == 0:
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local, 0] = a_pack[0]
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local, 1] = a_pack[1]
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local + 32, 0] = a_pack[2]
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local + 32, 1] = a_pack[3]
                else:
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local, 2] = a_pack[0]
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local, 3] = a_pack[1]
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local + 32, 2] = a_pack[2]
                    a_shared[0, a_tile, a_local + 32, 3] = a_pack[3]

            if tid >= 128:
                b_tid = tid - 128
                b_col = b_tid >> 1
                b_half = b_tid & 1
                b_tile = b_col >> 5
                b_local = b_col & 31
                b_offset = S.convert(((n0 + b_col) * INPUT_SIZE + next_k0 + b_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
                b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero_i32, b_offset, 0)
                if b_half == 0:
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local, 0] = b_pack[0]
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local, 1] = b_pack[1]
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local + 32, 0] = b_pack[2]
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local + 32, 1] = b_pack[3]
                else:
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local, 2] = b_pack[0]
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local, 3] = b_pack[1]
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local + 32, 2] = b_pack[2]
                    b_shared[0, b_tile, b_local + 32, 3] = b_pack[3]

            a_frag1 = S.view(a_shared[1, warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
            b_frag1 = S.view(b_shared[1, warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
            c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], c_lane)
            c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[1], b_frag1[1], c_lane)

            next_k1 = (k_pair + 1) * K_PAIR_TILES + TILE_K
            if tid < 128:
                a_row = tid >> 1
                a_half = tid & 1
                a_tile = a_row >> 5
                a_local = a_row & 31
                a_offset = S.convert(((block_row + a_row) * INPUT_SIZE + next_k1 + a_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
                a_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(x_rsrc, zero_i32, a_offset, 0)
                if a_half == 0:
                    a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local, 0] = a_pack[0]
                    a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local, 1] = a_pack[1]
                    a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local + 32, 0] = a_pack[2]
                    a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local + 32, 1] = a_pack[3]
                else:
                    a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local, 2] = a_pack[0]
                    a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local, 3] = a_pack[1]
                    a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local + 32, 2] = a_pack[2]
                    a_shared[1, a_tile, a_local + 32, 3] = a_pack[3]

            if tid >= 128:
                b_tid = tid - 128
                b_col = b_tid >> 1
                b_half = b_tid & 1
                b_tile = b_col >> 5
                b_local = b_col & 31
                b_offset = S.convert(((n0 + b_col) * INPUT_SIZE + next_k1 + b_half * 8) * 2, S.i32)
                b_pack = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(w_rsrc, zero_i32, b_offset, 0)
                if b_half == 0:
                    b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local, 0] = b_pack[0]
                    b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local, 1] = b_pack[1]
                    b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local + 32, 0] = b_pack[2]
                    b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local + 32, 1] = b_pack[3]
                else:
                    b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local, 2] = b_pack[0]
                    b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local, 3] = b_pack[1]
                    b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local + 32, 2] = b_pack[2]
                    b_shared[1, b_tile, b_local + 32, 3] = b_pack[3]

            S.syncthreads()

        a_frag0 = S.view(a_shared[0, warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        b_frag0 = S.view(b_shared[0, warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[0], b_frag0[0], c_lane)
        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag0[1], b_frag0[1], c_lane)

        a_frag1 = S.view(a_shared[1, warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        b_frag1 = S.view(b_shared[1, warp_col, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))
        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[0], b_frag1[0], c_lane)
        c_lane = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag1[1], b_frag1[1], c_lane)

        local_col = warp_col * 32 + (lane & 31)
        global_col = n0 + local_col
        bias = S.convert(BIAS0[global_col], S.f32)
        row_lane_bit = lane >> 5

        for slot in S.range(16):
            local_row = warp_row * 32 + (slot & 3) + 4 * row_lane_bit + 8 * (slot >> 2)
            value = c_lane[slot] + bias
            sigmoid = one_f32 / (one_f32 + S.exp(-value))
            c_shared[local_row, local_col] = sigmoid

        S.syncthreads()

        if tid < TILE_M:
            partial = row_sums[tid]
            for col in S.range(TILE_N):
                partial += c_shared[tid, col]
            row_sums[tid] = partial

        S.syncthreads()

    if tid < TILE_M:
        Y[block_row + tid, 0] = S.convert(row_sums[tid], S.bf16)


class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, input_size, hidden_size):
        super().__init__()
        self.linear = nn.Linear(input_size, hidden_size)
        self._weight_cache = None
        self._weight_key = None
        self._bias_cache = None
        self._bias_key = None

    def _maybe_refresh_cache(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> tuple[torch.Tensor, torch.Tensor]:
        weight = self.linear.weight
        bias = self.linear.bias
        weight_key = (weight.data_ptr(), weight._version, x.device, torch.bfloat16)
        bias_key = (bias.data_ptr(), bias._version, x.device, torch.bfloat16)

+                else:

             S.syncthreads()
 
+        a_frag0 = S.view(a_shared[0, warp_row, lane], S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

         global_col = n0 + local_col
         bias = S.convert(BIAS0[global_col], S.f32)

codex
Implemented the updated kernel in [output_model_new.py](/workspace/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb2/p56/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round2/output_model_new.py).

The kernel keeps the 4-wave 2x2 warp-grid MFMA structure, stages A/B through LDS with `raw_buffer_load_x4`, and unrolls the K loop by 2 using two LDS stages per iteration. I kept the cudagraph-safe parameter caching path in `ModelNew.forward()`.

I was not able to obtain a completed harness result from the required evaluation command. The command repeatedly stayed active without producing output or writing `debug_eval.jsonl`, so I do not have a correctness-pass artifact to report.
